whoever/quiconque, qui que ce soit/She promised to help whoever came to her with a genuine need for guidance.
glances/regards, coups d'œil, jette un coup d'œil/She always glances up from her work whenever someone enters the room.
righteous/juste, vertueux, irréprochable/She had a very strong and deeply felt sense of righteous indignation at injustice.
dash/tiret, élan, foncer, pointe/She made a sudden dash for the door when she heard the wonderful news.
horns/cornes, klaxons, cors/She heard the sound of hunting horns echoing distantly across the misty morning fields.
decisive/décisif, déterminant, résolu/She made a very decisive and very final decision that surprised everyone around her.
stooped/se pencha, courbé, voûté/She stooped to pick up the small and very beautiful flower from the path.
intimacy/intimité, familiarité/She valued the deep intimacy of very close and long-standing friendships above all else.
pan/poêle, casserole, critiquer/She placed the old pan on the stove and began to cook the simple meal.
preference/préférence, penchant/Her strong preference was always for simplicity and clarity over any kind of complexity.
accepts/accepte, admet/She graciously accepts all forms of praise and constructive criticism with equal measure.
blaze/flamme, feu, éclat, brûler/She felt the warm blaze of the fire on her face as she sat reading.
pool/piscine, mare, pool, mettre en commun/She sat beside the still garden pool and watched the evening reflections.
